<h2 class="linkro-darkred">
<a href="/news/article-2131060/Leopard-plays-baby-antelope-South-African-bush-happy-ending.html">Don't play with your food: What happened when a leopard befriended a cute baby antelope? (Actually, you probably don't want to know)</a>
</h2>
<div class="articletext">
<a href="/news/article-2131060/Leopard-plays-baby-antelope-South-African-bush-happy-ending.html" rel="nofollow">
<img src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2012/04/17/article-2131060-12A3E1CC000005DC-957_964x298.jpg" alt="leopard" width="964" height="298" />
</a>
<div >
<p>
The leopard played with the calf for 45 minutes and the small creature was so unafraid of the predator it even tried to suckle milk from it. The leggy calf, which in one picture bares similarity to the character Bambi, sat in between the leopards paws fearlessly and pranced around before the big cat got bored and hungry.
</p>
</div>	
</div>

<h2 class="linkro-darkred">
<a href="/news/article-2131290/Revealed-Official-fears-U-S-UK-President-Obamas-anti-American-anti-white-father.html">Revealed: How <br/>State Department officials feared <br/>President Obama's 'anti-American' father when he came to U.S.</a>
</h2>
<a href="/news/article-2131290/Revealed-Official-fears-U-S-UK-President-Obamas-anti-American-anti-white-father.html" rel="nofollow">
<img src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2012/04/18/article-2131290-025BC44E000005DC-217_308x227.jpg" alt="Father and son: The Barack Obamas together, when the US President was just 10 years old" width="308" height="227" />
</a>
<div class="articletext-holder">
<p>
Barack Obama Snr. was categorised with others as 'anti-American and anti-white' when he moved to the United States in 1959. Mr Obama Snr (pictured with his son) had grown up in Kenya under British rule and aroused the fears of colonial officers and U.S. officials when he won a chance to study in Hawaii. A diplomat wrote: 'I have discussed with the State Department. They point out that Kenya students have a bad reputation over here for falling into the wrong hands and for becoming both anti-American and anti-white.'
</p>

<ul class="article-icon-links cleared">

</a>
</li>

<h2 class="linkro-darkred">
<a href="/news/article-2131257/Warren-Buffett-says-early-prostate-cancer.html" class="js-link-clickable">Warren Buffett reveals he has early prostate cancer... but insists everything is fine </a>
</h2>
<div class="articletext">
<a href="/news/article-2131257/Warren-Buffett-says-early-prostate-cancer.html" rel="nofollow" class="js-link-clickable">
<img src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2012/04/17/article-2131257-12A47094000005DC-176_87x84.jpg" alt="Announcement: Warren Buffett's letter says he and his doctors have decided on a two-month treatment plan to begin in mid-July" width="87" height="84" />
</a>
<p>
Warren Buffett, the 81-year-old billionaire investor and CEO, says in an open letter, released Tuesday, that his condition is 'not remotely life-threatening' or debilitating.
</p>
</div>

<h2 class="linkro-darkred">
<a href="/news/article-2131019/Talk-embarrassing-Football-players-dad-knocks-schools-30-000-trophy.html" class="js-link-clickable">Talk about embarrassing! Football player's dad smashes school's $30,000 trophy after tripping on rug<br/></a>
</h2>
<div class="articletext">
<a href="/news/article-2131019/Talk-embarrassing-Football-players-dad-knocks-schools-30-000-trophy.html" rel="nofollow" class="js-link-clickable">
<img src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2012/04/17/article-2131019-12A2EB2F000005DC-637_87x84.jpg" alt="The Waterford Crystal Coaches' Trophy is valued at $30,000 and the University of Alabama's 2011 trophy was knocked over by a parent" width="87" height="84" />
</a>
<p>
The Waterford Crystal trophy designed in the shape of an elegant football was on display at the University of Alabama athletic facility when it came crashing down on Saturday.
</p>
</div>

<h2 class="linkro-darkred">
<a href="/news/article-2131179/John-Edwards-spotted-getting-12-95-haircut-SuperCuts.html">From a Beverly Hills salon to SuperCuts: Hard-up John Edwards forced to get a $12.95 haircut - eight years after blowing $1,250 on a single coif (but can you spot the difference?)</a>
</h2>
<div class="articletext">
<a href="/news/article-2131179/John-Edwards-spotted-getting-12-95-haircut-SuperCuts.html" rel="nofollow">
<img src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2012/04/17/article-2131179-12A45B49000005DC-455_636x383.jpg" alt="edwards" width="636" height="383" />
</a>
<div >
<p>
The disgraced vice presidential nominee got his haircut at a Raleigh, North Carolina SuperCuts- a far cry from his $400 cuts while on the 2004 and 2008 presidential campaigns. Now, as the jury selection process begins for his corruption trial in Raleigh, North Carolina, Edwards has downsized dramatically. 
</p>
</div>

<h2 class="linkro-darkred">
<a href="/news/article-2130909/Police-DNA-samples-schoolchildren-bid-solve-murder-girl-13-battered-stabbed-throttled-death.html" class="js-link-clickable">Police take DNA samples from schoolchildren in bid to solve murder of girl, 13, found battered, stabbed and throttled to death</a>
</h2>

It was seized in January 1968 and is now moored along the Taedong River in Pyongyang, North Korea." width="636" height="371" />
</a>
<div >
<p>
The USS Pueblo is the U.S. Navy's only ship that is held captive. The spying vessel was seized in January 1968 and is now moored along the Taedong River in Pyongyang, where it is open to visitors as a museum. Untouched since its capture, the vessel's structure is still riddled with bullet holes (pictured bottom) - a frightening reminder of the brutal takeover that left one crew member dead and more than 80 gagged and beaten before they were sent to POW camps.
</p>
</div>

<h2 class="linkro-darkred">
<a href="/news/article-2131117/He-pretty-look-does-bristly-mouse-hold-secret-cure-baldness.html">He may not be very pretty to look at but does this bristly mouse hold the secret cure to baldness AND grey hair? <br/></a>
</h2>
<div class="articletext">
<a href="/news/article-2131117/He-pretty-look-does-bristly-mouse-hold-secret-cure-baldness.html" rel="nofollow">
<img src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2012/04/17/article-2131117-12A2FBB6000005DC-677_636x372.jpg" alt="Hair he is: This picture shows tufts of hair grown from stem cells on the back of a bald mouse, which Japanese researchers have been testing to try and find a cure for baldness with coloured hairs" width="636" height="372" />
</a>
<div >
<p>
As if the thought of curing baldness wasn't exciting enough, Japanese scientists in Tokyo say they may also have found a way of saying goodbye to grey. In a two-in-one experiment, they have found a way of growing hair and of making it pigmented. Their success has been on mice but they hope to test the technique on men for the first time in as little as three years.
</p>

<h2 class="linkro-darkred">
<a href="/news/article-2131055/Final-survivors-WWII-Doolittle-Raid-Tokyo-toast-gone-70th-reunion-daring-air-strike.html">'We didn't know to be afraid': Five surviving vets from daring WWII Doolittle Raid on Tokyo gather on 70th anniversary and remember the 75 who have died</a>
</h2>
<div class="articletext">
<a href="/news/article-2131055/Final-survivors-WWII-Doolittle-Raid-Tokyo-toast-gone-70th-reunion-daring-air-strike.html" rel="nofollow">
<img src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2012/04/17/article-2131055-12A35FDF000005DC-560_636x380.jpg" alt="Doolittle" width="636" height="380" />
</a>
<div >
<p>
A ceremony to be held tomorrow near Dayton, Ohio, will come 70 years to the day after the bombing raid over Tokyo led by Lt. Col. 'Jimmy' Doolittle, right, that helped change the course of World War II. Five men - the last alive of the original Doolittle's Raiders - pictured in 2007, left, will help remember the dead by reading the 75 names engraved on silver goblets.
</p>
</div>
